                    <th class="Table__TH" title="">
                     <span class="underline" title="Adjusted Total Quarterback Rating, which values the quarterback on all play types on a 0-100 scale adjusted for the strength of opposing defenses faced.">
                      <a class="AnchorLink clr-gray-01" href="/nfl/qbr/_/sort/schedAdjQBR/dir/asc" tabindex="0">
                       QBR
                       <svg class="ArrowIcon__TableSort icon__svg" style="display:inline-block;height:10px;width:10px;margin-left:4px" viewbox="0 0 24 24">
                        <use xlink:href="#icon__caret__down">
                        </use>
                       </svg>
                      </a>
                     </span>
                    </th>
                    <th class="Table__TH" title="">
                     <span class="underline" title="Number of points contributed by a quarterback, accounting for QBR and how much he plays, above the level of an average quarterback.">
                      <a class="AnchorLink clr-gray-01" href="/nfl/qbr/_/sort/qbpaa/dir/desc" tabindex="0">
                       PAA
                      </a>
                     </span>
                    </th>
                    <th class="Table__TH" title="">
                     <span class="underline" title="Plays on which the QB has a non-zero expected points contribution. Includes most plays that are not handoffs.">
                      <a class="AnchorLink clr-gray-01" href="/nfl/qbr/_/sort/actionPlays/dir/desc" tabindex="0">
                       PLAYS
                      </a>
                     </span>
                    </th>
                    <th class="Table__TH" title="">
                     <span class="underline" title="Total expected points added with low leverage plays, according to ESPN Win Probability model, down-weighted.">
                      <a class="AnchorLink clr-gray-01" href="/nfl/qbr/_/sort/cwepaTotal/dir/desc" tabindex="0">
                       EPA
                      </a>
                     </span>
                    </th>
                    <th class="Table__TH" title="">
                     <span class="underline" title="Expected points added on pass attempts with low leverage plays down-weighted.">
                      <a class="AnchorLink clr-gray-01" href="/nfl/qbr/_/sort/cwepaPassesCondensed/dir/desc" tabindex="0">
                       PASS
                      </a>
                     </span>
                    </th>
                    <th class="Table__TH" title="">
                     <span class="underline" title="Clutch-weighted expected points added through rushes">
                      <a class="AnchorLink clr-gray-01" href="/nfl/qbr/_/sort/cwepaRuns/dir/desc" tabindex="0">
                       RUN
                      </a>
                     </span>
                    </th>
                    <th class="Table__TH" title="">
                     <span class="underline" title="Expected points added on sacks with low leverage plays down-weighted.">
                      <a class="AnchorLink clr-gray-01" href="/nfl/qbr/_/sort/cwepaSackedCondensed/dir/desc" tabindex="0">
                       SACK
                      </a>
                     </span>
                    </th>
                    <th class="Table__TH" title="">
                     <span class="underline" title="Expected points added on penalties with low leverage plays down-weighted.">
                      <a class="AnchorLink clr-gray-01" href="/nfl/qbr/_/sort/cwepaPenalties/dir/desc" tabindex="0">
                       PEN
                      </a>
                     </span>
                    </th>
                    <th class="Table__TH" title="">
                     <span class="underline" title="Raw Total Quarterback Rating, which values quarterback on all play types on a 0-100 scale (not adjusted for opposing defenses faced)">

                       RAW
                      </a>
                     </span>
                    </th>
